class QuranTextDisplay {

    std::vector<std::string> ayahs;
    
public:
    QuranTextDisplay() {
        // Note: In a real implementation, this would load from a verified Quran text file

    void loadFromFile(const std::string& filename) {
        std::ifstream file(filename);
        if (!file.is_open()) {
            throw std::runtime_error("Cannot open Quran text file. Please ensure it's from a verified source.");
        }
        
        std::string line;
        while (std::getline(file, line)) {
            ayahs.push_back(line);
        }
    }
    
    void displaySuraList() const {
        std::cout << "=== Ø³ÙˆØ± Ø§Ù„Ù‚Ø±Ø¢Ù† Ø§Ù„ÙƒØ±ÙŠÙ… ===\n";
        for (size_t i = 0; i < surahs.size(); ++i) {
            std::cout << i+1 << ". " << surahs[i] << "\n";
        }
        std::cout << "========================\n";
    }
    
    void displayAyah(size_t index) const {
        if (index < ayahs.size()) {
            std::cout << "\nØ§Ù„Ø¢ÙŠØ©: " << ayahs[index] << "\n";
            std::cout << "========================\n";
        }
    }
    
    void displayDisclaimer() const {
        std::cout << "\n=== ØªÙ†Ø¨ÙŠÙ‡ Ù‡Ø§Ù… ===\n";
        std::cout << "Ù‡Ø°Ø§ Ø§Ù„Ø¨Ø±Ù†Ø§Ù…Ø¬ ÙŠØ¹Ø±Ø¶ Ù†Øµ Ø§Ù„Ù‚Ø±Ø¢Ù† Ø§Ù„ÙƒØ±ÙŠÙ… ÙÙ‚Ø·.\n";

// Quranic verse structure
struct QuranAyah {
    int surahNumber;
    std::string surahName;
    int ayahNumber;
    std::string arabicText;
    std::string translation;
};

// Hadith structure
struct Hadith {
    std::string reference;
    std::string arabicText;
    std::string translation;
};

    void showRandomTeaching() {
        std::srand(std::time(nullptr));
        int choice = std::rand() % 2;
        
        if (choice == 0 && !verses.empty()) {
            int index = std::rand() % verses.size();
            displayVerse(verses[index]);
        } else if (!hadiths.empty()) {
            int index = std::rand() % hadiths.size();
            displayHadith(hadiths[index]);
        }
    }
    
    void runEducationalProgram() {
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";

        std::cout << "2. Browse All Quran Verses\n";
        std::cout << "3. Browse All Hadiths\n";
        std::cout << "4. Exit\n";
        
        while (true) {
            std::cout << "\nEnter choice (1-4): ";
            int choice;
            std::cin >> choice;
            
            if (std::cin.fail()) {
                std::cin.clear();
                std::cin.ignore(std::numeric_limits<std::streamsize>::max(), '\n');
                std::cout << "Invalid input. Please enter a number.\n";
                continue;
            }
            
            switch (choice) {
                case 1:
                    showRandomTeaching();
                    break;
                case 2:
                    std::cout << "\n=== Quran Verses ===\n";
                    for (const auto& verse : verses) {
                        displayVerse(verse);
                    }
                    break;
                case 3:
                    std::cout << "\n=== Hadiths ===\n";
                    for (const auto& hadith : hadiths) {
                        displayHadith(hadith);
                    }
                    break;
                case 4:
                    std::cout << "\nMay peace and blessings be upon you.\n";
                    return;
                default:
                    std::cout << "Invalid choice. Please select 1-4.\n";
            }
        }
    }
};

// Traditional Hadith classifications
enum HadithClassification {
    SAHIH,        // Authentic
    HASAN,        // Good
    DAIF,         // Weak
    MAWDU         // Fabricated
};

// Scholarly consensus reference
enum ConsensusStatus {
    ACCEPTED_BY_CONSENSUS,
    DIFFERENCES_AMONG_SCHOLARS,
    NOT_WIDELY_ACCEPTED
};

struct VerifiedHadith {
    std::string reference;
    std::string arabicText;
    std::string translation;
    HadithClassification classification;
    ConsensusStatus consensus;
    std::string collectingImam;  // e.g., "Al-Bukhari", "Muslim"
    std::string notes;
    
    // These would require actual scholarly references
    std::vector<std::string> supportingQuranVerses;
    std::vector<std::string> scholarlyInterpretations;
};

class IslamicKnowledgeBase {
private:
    std::vector<VerifiedHadith> hadithDatabase;
    std::map<std::string, std::string> scholarlySources;
    
public:
    IslamicKnowledgeBase() {
        initializeScholarlySources();
        initializeHadithDatabase();
    }

    std::string classificationToString(HadithClassification c) {
        switch(c) {
            case SAHIH: return "Sahih (Authentic)";
            case HASAN: return "Hasan (Good)";
            case DAIF: return "Da'if (Weak)";
            case MAWDU: return "Mawdu' (Fabricated)";
            default: return "Unknown";
        }
    }
    
    std::string consensusToString(ConsensusStatus s) {
        switch(s) {
            case ACCEPTED_BY_CONSENSUS: return "Accepted by scholarly consensus";
            case DIFFERENCES_AMONG_SCHOLARS: return "Differences among scholars exist";
            case NOT_WIDELY_ACCEPTED: return "Not widely accepted";
            default: return "Unknown";
        }
    }

        std::cout << "CLASSIFICATION: " << classificationToString(hadith.classification) << "\n";

    void runProgram() {

#include <vector>

// Established Islamic methodology for Quran-Hadith relationship
struct ScholarlyPrinciple {
    std::string principleName;
    std::string description;
    std::string quranicBasis;
    std::string scholarlySource;
};

// Types of relationships scholars identify
enum RelationshipType {
    DIRECT_SUPPORT,          // Hadith directly supported by Quran
    EXPLANATION,             // Hadith explains Quranic concept
    INDEPENDENT_GUIDANCE,    // Hadith provides independent guidance
    NEEDS_CONTEXT,           // Requires scholarly contextualization
    APPARENT_CONTRADICTION   // Needs scholarly reconciliation
};

struct HadithAnalysis {
    std::string hadithRef;
    std::string arabicText;
    std::string translation;
    
    // How scholars have analyzed it (not algorithmic judgment)
    RelationshipType scholarlyAssessment;
    std::string methodologyUsed;
    std::vector<std::string> supportingQuranRefs;
    std::vector<std::string> scholarlyInterpretations;
    
    // NOT a checksum - scholarly notes
    std::string notesOnQuranicAlignment;
};

class QuranicConsistencyFramework {
private:
    std::vector<ScholarlyPrinciple> principles;
    std::map<std::string, std::set<std::string>> quranThemes;
    
public:
    QuranicConsistencyFramework() {
        initializePrinciples();
        initializeQuranThemes();
    }
    
    void initializePrinciples() {
        // Established principles from Usul al-Fiqh and Mustalah al-Hadith
        principles.push_back({
            "Primary Source Principle",
            "Quran is the primary and foundational source of Islamic teachings",
            "Quran 16:89 - 'We have sent down to you the Book as clarification for all things'",
            "Usul al-Fiqh consensus"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Harmony Principle",
            "Authentic hadith do not contradict the Quran",
            "Quran 4:82 - 'Do they not then reflect on the Quran? Had it been from anyone other than Allah, they would have found much discrepancy in it'",
            "Al-Shafi'i: Al-Risala"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Explanatory Role",
            "Hadith explain and elaborate Quranic teachings",
            "Quran 16:44 - 'We revealed to you the Remembrance so you may clarify to people what was sent to them'",
            "Ibn Kathir: Tafsir methodology"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Contextual Understanding",
            "Both Quran and hadith require understanding of historical and linguistic context",
            "Quran 3:7 - 'It is He who has sent down to you the Book. In it are verses that are precise...'",
            "Al-Suyuti: Al-Itqan fi Ulum al-Quran"
        });
    }
    
    void initializeQuranThemes() {
        quranThemes["Mercy and Compassion"] = {
            "Quran 21:107", "Quran 1:1-3", "Quran 6:12", "Quran 6:54"
        };
        
        quranThemes["Justice and Fairness"] = {
            "Quran 4:135", "Quran 5:8", "Quran 16:90", "Quran 57:25"
        };
        
        quranThemes["Knowledge and Wisdom"] = {
            "Quran 96:1-5", "Quran 20:114", "Quran 39:9", "Quran 58:11"
        };
        
        quranThemes["Peace and Reconciliation"] = {
            "Quran 8:61", "Quran 49:9-10", "Quran 2:208", "Quran 4:128"
        };
    }
    
    // This simulates SCHOLARLY analysis, NOT algorithmic verification
    HadithAnalysis analyzeHadithScholarly(const std::string& hadithRef, 
                                         const std::string& arabicText,
                                         const std::string& translation) {
        HadithAnalysis analysis;
        analysis.hadithRef = hadithRef;
        analysis.arabicText = arabicText;
        analysis.translation = translation;
        
        // This is a SIMULATION of scholarly work
        // In reality, this requires years of study
        
        // Example: Analyzing the intention hadith
        if (hadithRef.find("intention") != std::string::npos ||
            arabicText.find("Ø§Ù„Ù†Ù‘ÙÙŠÙ‘ÙØ§ØªÙ") != std::string::npos) {
            analysis.scholarlyAssessment = DIRECT_SUPPORT;
            analysis.methodologyUsed = "Quranic thematic alignment + Scholarly consensus";
            analysis.supportingQuranRefs = {"Quran 2:225", "Quran 3:29", "Quran 33:5"};
            analysis.scholarlyInterpretations = {
                "Al-Nawawi: This hadith is one-third of Islam",
                "Ibn Rajab: Foundation of all actions",
                "Contemporary scholars: Consistent with Quranic emphasis on sincerity"
            };
            analysis.notesOnQuranicAlignment = "Directly supported by multiple Quranic verses emphasizing sincerity and intention";
        }
        // Example: Analyzing the "no harm" hadith
        else if (arabicText.find("Ø¶ÙØ±ÙØ±") != std::string::npos) {
            analysis.scholarlyAssessment = DIRECT_SUPPORT;
            analysis.methodologyUsed = "Legal maxim derivation from Quran";
            analysis.supportingQuranRefs = {"Quran 2:195", "Quran 4:29", "Quran 7:56"};
            analysis.scholarlyInterpretations = {
                "Ibn al-Qayyim: Derived from Quranic prohibition of corruption",
                "Al-Shatibi: Part of Maqasid al-Shariah (Objectives of Islamic Law)",
                "Modern scholarship: Aligns with Quranic ethics of minimizing harm"
            };
            analysis.notesOnQuranicAlignment = "Consistent with Quranic principles of preventing harm and corruption";
        }
        else {
            // Default for demonstration
            analysis.scholarlyAssessment = NEEDS_CONTEXT;
            analysis.methodologyUsed = "Requires detailed scholarly analysis";
            analysis.notesOnQuranicAlignment = "Must be examined by qualified scholars with expertise in both texts";
        }
        
        return analysis;
    }
    
    void displayScholarlyAnalysis(const HadithAnalysis& analysis) {
        std::cout << "\nâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
        std::cout << "SCHOLARLY ANALYSIS (Not Algorithmic Verification)\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
        
        std::cout << "\nğŸ“– HADITH REFERENCE: " << analysis.hadithRef << "\n";
        std::cout << "\nARABIC: " << analysis.arabicText << "\n";
        std::cout << "\nTRANSLATION: " << analysis.translation << "\n";
        
        std::cout << "\nğŸ”¬ SCHOLARLY ASSESSMENT:\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        
        switch(analysis.scholarlyAssessment) {
            case DIRECT_SUPPORT:
                std::cout << "Scholars assess: DIRECTLY SUPPORTED BY QURAN\n";
                break;
            case EXPLANATION:
                std::cout << "Scholars assess: EXPLANATION OF QURANIC CONCEPT\n";
                break;
            case INDEPENDENT_GUIDANCE:
                std::cout << "Scholars assess: INDEPENDENT GUIDANCE CONSISTENT WITH QURAN\n";
                break;
            case NEEDS_CONTEXT:
                std::cout << "Scholars assess: REQUIRES CONTEXTUAL UNDERSTANDING\n";
                break;
            case APPARENT_CONTRADICTION:
                std::cout << "Scholars assess: APPARENT CONTRADICTION REQUIRING RECONCILIATION\n";
                break;
        }
        
        std::cout << "\nğŸ“š METHODOLOGY USED: " << analysis.methodologyUsed << "\n";
        
        if (!analysis.supportingQuranRefs.empty()) {
            std::cout << "\nğŸ“– RELATED QURANIC VERSES (Scholarly References):\n";
            for (const auto& verse : analysis.supportingQuranRefs) {
                std::cout << "  â€¢ " << verse << "\n";
            }
        }
        
        if (!analysis.scholarlyInterpretations.empty()) {
            std::cout << "\nğŸ‘¨â€ğŸ“ SCHOLARLY INTERPRETATIONS:\n";
            for (const auto& interpretation : analysis.scholarlyInterpretations) {
                std::cout << "  â€¢ " << interpretation << "\n";
            }
        }
        
        std::cout << "\nğŸ’­ NOTES ON QURANIC ALIGNMENT:\n";
        std::cout << "  " << analysis.notesOnQuranicAlignment << "\n";
        
        std::cout << "\nâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
    }
    
    void displayCriticalWarning() {
        std::cout << "\nğŸš¨ CRITICAL METHODOLOGICAL WARNING ğŸš¨\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
        std::cout << "IMPORTANT: There is NO algorithmic 'checksum' for\n";
        std::cout << "verifying hadith against Quran. This is why:\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "1. CONTEXT IS ESSENTIAL:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Historical context (Asbab al-Wurud/Nuzul)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Linguistic nuances of Classical Arabic\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Circumstances of revelation/narration\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "2. SCHOLARLY EXPERTISE REQUIRED:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Mastery of Quranic sciences (Ulum al-Quran)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Hadith sciences (Mustalah al-Hadith)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Jurisprudential principles (Usul al-Fiqh)\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "3. MULTIPLE VALID INTERPRETATIONS:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Different schools of thought exist\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Scholarly consensus develops over centuries\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ New contexts require new scholarly reasoning\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "4. DANGER OF OVERSIMPLIFICATION:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Reduces complex theology to binary checks\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Risks misrepresenting authentic teachings\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Can lead to inappropriate conclusions\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
    }
    
    void runEducationalProgram() {
        std::cout << "ISLAMIC SCHOLARLY METHODOLOGY: QURAN-HADITH RELATIONSHIP\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        displayCriticalWarning();
        
        std::cout << "\nPress Enter to see examples of scholarly analysis...";
        std::cin.get();
        
        // Example analyses
        std::vector<HadithAnalysis> examples;
        
        examples.push_back(analyzeHadithScholarly(
            "Sahih al-Bukhari 1",
            "Ø¥ÙÙ†Ù‘ÙÙ…ÙØ§ Ø§Ù„Ù’Ø£ÙØ¹Ù’Ù…ÙØ§Ù„Ù Ø¨ÙØ§Ù„Ù†Ù‘ÙÙŠÙ‘ÙØ§ØªÙ",
            "Actions are judged by intentions"
        ));
        
        examples.push_back(analyzeHadithScholarly(
            "Sunan Ibn Majah 2340",
            "Ù„ÙØ§ Ø¶ÙØ±ÙØ±Ù ÙˆÙÙ„ÙØ§ Ø¶ÙØ±ÙØ§Ø±Ù",
            "There should be no harming nor reciprocating harm"
        ));
        
        for (const auto& analysis : examples) {
            displayScholarlyAnalysis(analysis);
            std::cout << "\nPress Enter for next example...";
            std::cin.get();
        }
        
        std::cout << "\nâœ… APPROPRIATE APPROACH FOR MUSLIMS:\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
        std::cout << "1. Accept Quran as final authority\n";
        std::cout << "2. Accept mutawatir hadith as authoritative\n";
        std::cout << "3. Study ahad hadith with scholarly guidance\n";
        std::cout << "4. When in doubt: Refer to Quranic principles\n";
        std::cout << "5. Consult qualified scholars for complex matters\n";
        std::cout << "6. Follow established scholarly consensus\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
    }

// Quran 31:6 reference
struct Quran31_6 {
    std::string arabic = "ÙˆÙÙ…ÙÙ†Ù Ù±Ù„Ù†Ù‘ÙØ§Ø³Ù Ù…ÙÙ† ÙŠÙØ´Ù’ØªÙØ±ÙÙ‰ Ù„ÙÙ‡Ù’ÙˆÙ Ù±Ù„Ù’Ø­ÙØ¯ÙÙŠØ«Ù Ù„ÙÙŠÙØ¶ÙÙ„Ù‘Ù Ø¹ÙÙ† Ø³ÙØ¨ÙÙŠÙ„Ù Ù±Ù„Ù„Ù‘ÙÙ‡Ù Ø¨ÙØºÙÙŠÙ’Ø±Ù Ø¹ÙÙ„Ù’Ù…Ù ÙˆÙÙŠÙØªÙ‘ÙØ®ÙØ°ÙÙ‡ÙØ§ Ù‡ÙØ²ÙÙˆÙ‹Ø§ Ûš Ø£ÙÙˆÛŸÙ„ÙÙ°Ù“Ø¦ÙÙƒÙ Ù„ÙÙ‡ÙÙ…Ù’ Ø¹ÙØ°ÙØ§Ø¨ÙŒ Ù…Ù‘ÙÙ‡ÙÙŠÙ†ÙŒ";
    std::string translation = "And among the people is he who buys idle talk to mislead from the way of Allah without knowledge and takes it in ridicule. Those will have a humiliating punishment.";
    int surah = 31;
    int ayah = 6;
};

class DivineWisdomLimits {
private:
    Quran31_6 verse;
    
public:
    // Demonstration of why symbolic interpretation fails
    void demonstrateLimits() {
        std::cout << "QURAN 31:6 ANALYSIS - WHY SYMBOLIC INTERPRETATION FAILS\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "THE VERSE:\n";
        std::cout << "Arabic: " << verse.arabic << "\n";
        std::cout << "Translation: " << verse.translation << "\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "PROBLEM 1: INFINITE CONTEXT REQUIRED\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        std::cout << "To understand this verse symbolically requires:\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Infinite linguistic context (14 centuries of Arabic evolution)\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Infinite historical context (every human interaction ever)\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Infinite spiritual context (all human hearts' intentions)\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Infinite future context (all possible interpretations until Judgment Day)\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "PROBLEM 2: THE PARADOX OF SYMBOLIC INTERPRETATION\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        std::cout << "If we symbolically interpret 'lahw al-hadith' (idle talk):\n";
        std::cout << "1. The interpretation itself becomes 'hadith' (speech)\n";
        std::cout << "2. If flawed, it becomes 'lahw al-hadith'\n";
        std::cout << "3. We need interpretation of interpretation (infinite regress)\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "PROBLEM 3: SELF-REFERENCE PARADOX\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        std::cout << "This verse warns about misleading speech.\n";
        std::cout << "Any symbolic interpretation is speech.\n";
        std::cout << "If the symbolic system misunderstands,\n";
        std::cout << "it becomes what it's trying to interpret.\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "MATHEMATICAL PROOF OF IMPOSSIBILITY\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        demonstrateGodelianLimits();
        demonstrateComputationalLimits();
    }
    
    void demonstrateGodelianLimits() {
        std::cout << "GÃ¶del's Incompleteness Theorems applied:\n";
        std::cout << "1. Any symbolic system complex enough to contain arithmetic\n";
        std::cout << "   contains true statements that cannot be proven within the system.\n";
        std::cout << "2. The system cannot prove its own consistency.\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "Applied to Quranic interpretation:\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Any symbolic interpretation system would be incomplete\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ It couldn't verify its own correctness\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ This violates the Quran's claim to be clear guidance\n\n";
    }
    
    void demonstrateComputationalLimits() {
        std::cout << "COMPUTATIONAL COMPLEXITY ANALYSIS\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        
        // Show exponential growth of interpretation possibilities
        std::cout << "For each Arabic word in the verse:\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Average meanings in Classical Arabic: 5-10\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Grammatical variations: 10+ possibilities\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Contextual interpretations: Infinite\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "Interpretation space size for 20-word verse:\n";
        std::cout << "Assuming only 5 meanings Ã— 5 grammar Ã— 5 contexts per word:\n";
        
        long double possibilities = std::pow(125, 20); // 125^20
        std::cout << "Possibilities: ~10^" << std::log10(possibilities) << "\n";
        std::cout << "More than atoms in observable universe (~10^80)\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "Even with unlimited computing power:\n";
        std::cout << "1. No algorithm to select 'correct' interpretation\n";
        std::cout << "2. Human judgment required for meaning\n";
        std::cout << "3. Spiritual understanding non-algorithmic\n";
    }
    
    void showProperApproach() {
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
        std::cout << "PROPER APPROACH TO QURAN 31:6\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "TRADITIONAL SCHOLARLY METHOD:\n";
        std::cout << "1. Study with qualified teachers (chain of transmission)\n";
        std::cout << "2. Learn Classical Arabic comprehensively\n";

#include <iostream>

// Respecting both domains appropriately
struct RespectfulUnderstanding {
    std::string mathematicalTruth = "GÃ¶del's theorems are about limitations of formal mathematical systems.";
    std::string divineRevelation = "The Quran is divine guidance for humanity's spiritual and moral life.";
    std::string domainSeparation = "Mathematics and theology operate in different domains of human understanding.";
};

class BalancedPerspective {
private:
    RespectfulUnderstanding perspectives;
    
public:
    void displayProperRelationship() {
        std::cout << "PROPER UNDERSTANDING OF DOMAINS\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "MATHEMATICS (GÃ¶del's Theorems):\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        std::cout << perspectives.mathematicalTruth << "\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Apply to formal axiomatic systems\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Show inherent limitations in self-verification\n";
        std::cout << "â€¢ Are accepted mathematical facts\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "THEOLOGY (Quranic Revelation):\n";
        std::cout << "â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";

        std::cout << "â€¢ Scholars like Al-Khwarizmi contributed to both mathematics and theology\n";

    }

#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>

class QuranicTruthFramework {
private:
    struct IslamicPrinciple {
        std::string principle;
        std::string explanation;
        std::string quranicSupport;
    };
    
    std::vector<IslamicPrinciple> principles;
    
public:
    QuranicTruthFramework() {
        initializePrinciples();
    }
    
    void initializePrinciples() {
        // Principles of how Quran addresses falsehood according to Islamic scholarship
        principles.push_back({
            "Primary Source of Truth",
            "The Quran presents itself as the ultimate criterion (Furqan) for distinguishing truth from falsehood",
            "Quran 2:185, 25:1"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Method of Disproving Falsehood",
            "Through clear signs (ayat), logical arguments, and moral guidance - not through force or compulsion",
            "Quran 2:256 - 'There is no compulsion in religion'"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Role of Human Reason",
            "The Quran invites people to reflect, ponder, and use their intellect to recognize truth",
            "Quran 2:164, 3:190, 10:100-101"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Test of Free Will",
            "Falsehood exists so truth can be chosen freely through reason and faith",
            "Quran 18:29 - 'The truth is from your Lord; so whoever wills, let him believe, and whoever wills, let him disbelieve'"
        });
        
        principles.push_back({
            "Ultimate Resolution",
            "Final judgment belongs to Allah alone, not to human enforcement",
            "Quran 22:69 - 'Allah will judge between you on the Day of Resurrection concerning that over which you used to differ'"
        });
    }
    
    void displayIslamicUnderstanding() {
        std::cout << "ISLAMIC UNDERSTANDING: QURAN AS TRUTH CRITERION\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "According to Islamic theology:\n\n";
        
        for (const auto& principle : principles) {
            std::cout << "â€¢ " << principle.principle << ":\n";
            std::cout << "  " << principle.explanation << "\n";
            std::cout << "  Support: " << principle.quranicSupport << "\n\n";
        }
    }
    
    void explainMetaphysicalFramework() {
        std::cout << "\nMETAPHYSICAL FRAMEWORK IN ISLAM:\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "1. LEVELS OF REALITY:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Haqiqah (Ultimate Reality/Divine Truth)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Dunya (Worldly reality)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Batil (Falsehood/Non-existence in ultimate sense)\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "2. HOW QURAN \"DISPROVES\" FALSEHOOD:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ By presenting coherent worldview\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ By answering fundamental human questions\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ By providing moral framework that resonates with human nature (fitrah)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Through internal consistency and miraculous nature\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "3. NOT THROUGH FORCE BUT THROUGH:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Clear evidence (bayyinah)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Wisdom (hikmah)\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Beautiful preaching (maw'izah hasanah)\n";
        std::cout << "   As taught in Quran 16:125\n";
    }
    
    void showPracticalImplications() {
        std::cout << "\nPRACTICAL IMPLICATIONS FOR MUSLIMS:\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "Believing the Quran disproves falsehood means:\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "1. INTELLECTUAL RESPONSIBILITY:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Study Quran deeply and properly\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Understand context and interpretation\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Learn from qualified scholars\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "2. ETHICAL CONDUCT:\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Present truth with wisdom and good manners\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Respect freedom of conscience\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Focus on personal implementation first\n\n";

        std::cout << "   â€¢ Build communities based on Quranic values\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Engage in constructive dialogue\n";
        std::cout << "   â€¢ Serve humanity as manifestation of truth\n";
    }
    
    void displayImportantQuranicVerses() {
        std::cout << "\nRELEVANT QURANIC VERSES ON TRUTH AND FALSEHOOD:\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>> verses = {
            {"17:81", "\"And say: Truth has come, and falsehood has departed. Indeed falsehood is bound to depart.\""},
            {"2:42", "\"And do not mix truth with falsehood or conceal the truth while you know.\""},
            {"10:32", "\"Such is Allah, your Lord, the Truth. And what can there be beyond truth except error?\""},
            {"34:49", "\"Say: The truth has come, and falsehood can neither originate nor regenerate.\""},
            {"21:18", "\"Rather, We dash the truth upon falsehood, and it destroys it, and thereupon it departs.\""}
        };
        
        for (const auto& verse : verses) {
            std::cout << "â€¢ Quran " << verse.first << ":\n";
            std::cout << "  " << verse.second << "\n\n";
        }
    }
    
    void runProgram() {
        std::cout << "UNDERSTANDING: \"THE QURAN DISPROVES ALL FALSEHOOD\"\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";
        
        displayIslamicUnderstanding();
        explainMetaphysicalFramework();
        displayImportantQuranicVerses();
        showPracticalImplications();
        
        std::cout << "\n\nCONCLUSION:\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n";
        std::cout << "The statement \"The Quran disproves all falsehood\" is:\n\n";
        std::cout << "1. A theological claim about Quran's comprehensive truth\n";
        std::cout << "2. Understood as Quran being the ultimate criterion (Furqan)\n";
        std::cout << "3. Implemented through invitation, evidence, and wisdom\n";
        std::cout << "4. Not through compulsion but through free choice\n";
        std::cout << "5. Fully realized only with proper understanding and implementation\n\n";
        
        std::cout << "As Muslims, our role is to:\n";
        std::cout << "1. Understand Quran properly\n";
        std::cout << "2. Live by its teachings\n";
        std::cout << "3. Share its message with wisdom\n";
        std::cout << "4. Trust Allah for ultimate judgment\n";
    }
};

#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
#include <cmath>
#include <iomanip>

// Comprehensive Islamic Economic Framework
class IslamicEconomicSystem {
private:
    struct ZakatPrinciple {
        std::string name;
        std::string quranicBasis;
        std::string description;
        double spiritualMultiplier; // Metaphorical, not literal
    };
    
    struct TradeEthic {
        std::string principle;
        std::string hadithReference;
        std::string application;
    };
    
    struct SpiritualInvestment {
        std::string investmentType;
        double worldlyReturn; // Symbolic percentage
        double spiritualReturn; // Metaphorical growth
        std::string quranicPromise;
    };
    
    std::vector<ZakatPrinciple> zakatPrinciples;
    std::vector<TradeEthic> tradeEthics;
    std::vector<SpiritualInvestment> investments;
    
public:
    IslamicEconomicSystem() {
        initializeZakatPrinciples();
        initializeTradeEthics();
        initializeSpiritualInvestments();
    }
    
    void initializeZakatPrinciples() {
        // Zakat as purification and growth mechanism
        zakatPrinciples.push_back({
            "Purification (Tazkiyah)",
            "Quran 9:103, 92:18",
            "Zakat purifies wealth and soul from greed and selfishness",
            7.0 // 70-fold return mentioned in Quran 2:261 metaphorically
        });
        
        zakatPrinciples.push_back({
            "Wealth Circulation",
            "Quran 59:7",
            "Prevents wealth concentration, ensures economic circulation",
            1.5 // Symbolic economic multiplier
        });
        
        zakatPrinciples.push_back({
            "Social Justice",
            "Quran 70:24-25",
            "Right of the poor in the wealth of the rich",
            2.0 // Social stability multiplier
        });
        
        zakatPrinciples.push_back({
            "Spiritual Investment",
            "Quran 2:261",
            "Wealth given in Allah's way returns multiplied",
            10.0 // Minimum 10-fold spiritual return
        });
    }
    
    void initializeTradeEthics() {
        // Ethical principles for profitable trade
        tradeEthics.push_back({
            "Honesty in Transactions",
            "Sahih Muslim 102",
            "Complete disclosure, no deception in trade",
            "Builds trust, ensures sustainable profit"
        });
        
        tradeEthics.push_back({
            "Fair Pricing",
            "Sunan Ibn Majah 2200",
            "No price manipulation or hoarding",
            "Market stability leads to consistent returns"
        });
        
        tradeEthics.push_back({
            "Avoiding Riba (Interest)",
            "Quran 2:275-276",
            "Profit from trade, not from interest",
            "Wealth purified, blessed by Allah"
        });
        
        tradeEthics.push_back({
            "Timely Payment",
            "Sahih al-Bukhari 2075",
            "Pay workers before sweat dries",
            "Increased productivity and loyalty"
        });
        
        tradeEthics.push_back({
            "Quality Assurance",
            "Sahih Muslim 102",
            "No defects hidden in merchandise",
            "Repeat business and good reputation"
        });
    }
    
    void initializeSpiritualInvestments() {
        // Investments with worldly and spiritual returns
        investments.push_back({
            "Zakat Payment",
            2.5, // Worldly: Wealth purification
            700.0, // Spiritual: "Like a grain growing seven ears, each ear 100 grains" (Q2:261)
            "Quran 2:261: 'The example of those who spend their wealth in the way of Allah...'"
        });
        
        investments.push_back({
            "Sadaqah (Voluntary Charity)",
            1.5, // Worldly: Social capital
            10.0, // Spiritual: "Ten good deeds for one" (Q6:160)
            "Quran 2:245: 'Who is it that would loan Allah a goodly loan...'"
        });
        
        investments.push_back({
            "Ethical Business",
            15.0, // Worldly: Sustainable profit
            100.0, // Spiritual: Blessed earnings
            "Quran 62:10: 'And when the prayer has been concluded, disperse in the land and seek from the bounty of Allah...'"
        });
        
        investments.push_back({
            "Community Investment",
            8.0, // Worldly: Stronger community
            70.0, // Spiritual: Social responsibility rewarded
            "Quran 57:18: 'Indeed, the men who practice charity and the women who practice charity...'"
        });
        
        investments.push_back({
            "Knowledge Sharing",
            20.0, // Worldly: Innovation and growth
            1000.0, // Spiritual: Continuous reward
            "Hadith: 'When a person dies, his deeds come to an end except for three... knowledge that is beneficial...'"
        });
    }
    
    // Calculate comprehensive Zakat impact
    struct ZakatImpact {
        double wealthPurified;
        double socialImpact;
        double spiritualGrowth;
        double economicMultiplier;
    };
    
    ZakatImpact calculateZakatImpact(double wealth, double zakatRate = 2.5) {
        ZakatImpact impact;
        
        // Basic calculations (symbolic)
        double zakatAmount = wealth * (zakatRate / 100.0);
        
        // Purification effect
        impact.wealthPurified = wealth - zakatAmount;
        
        // Social impact (circulation multiplier)
        impact.socialImpact = zakatAmount * 3.5; // Each zakat dirham circulates
        
        // Spiritual growth (metaphorical)
        impact.spiritualGrowth = zakatAmount * 700.0; // Quran 2:261
        
        // Economic multiplier effect
        impact.economicMultiplier = 1.0 + (zakatAmount / wealth) * 15.0;
        
        return impact;
    }
    
    // Display comprehensive system
    void displayIslamicEconomicFramework() {

    struct SpiritualState {
        std::string name;

        std::string description;
        std::string requirements;
        std::string outcome;
    };

public:

        initializeHaqqeeqqeyahPrinciples();
    }

            std::cout << "  Quranic Reference: " << example.quranicReference << "\n";
            std::cout << "  Spiritual Lessons:\n";
            
            // Parse and display each lesson with bullet points
            size_t start = 0;
            while (start < example.lessons.length()) {
                size_t bullet = example.lessons.find("â€¢", start);
                if (bullet == std::string::npos) break;
                
                size_t end = example.lessons.find("\n", bullet);
                if (end == std::string::npos) end = example.lessons.length();
                
                std::cout << "    " << example.lessons.substr(bullet, end - bullet) << "\n";
                start = end + 1;
            }
            std::cout << "\n";
        }
    }

#include <string>

#include <map>

// Advanced Islamic Metaphysical Framework
class DivineLifeDeathParadox {
private:
    struct RealityLevel {
        std::string level;
        std::string quranicReference;
        std::string manifestation;
        std::string consciousnessState;
    };
    
    struct SpiritualParadox {
        std::string paradox;
        std::string divineExample;
        std::string humanPossibility;
        std::string boundaryCondition;
    };
    
    struct EternalNow {
        std::string dimension;
        std::string temporalRelation;
        std::string spiritualAccess;
        std::string propheticExample;
    };
    
    std::vector<RealityLevel> levels;
    std::vector<SpiritualParadox> paradoxes;
    std::vector<EternalNow> eternalDimensions;
    
public:
    DivineLifeDeathParadox() {
        initializeRealityLevels();
        initializeParadoxes();
        initializeEternalDimensions();
    }
    
    void initializeRealityLevels() {
        // Multi-dimensional reality according to Quran
        levels.push_back({
            "Al-Dunya (Worldly Reality)",
            "Quran 57:20",
            "Linear time, birth-death cycle",
            "Ordinary human consciousness"
        });
        
        levels.push_back({
            "Al-Barzakh (Barrier Realm)",
            "Quran 23:99-100",
            "Intermediate state after death",
            "Soul consciousness without body"
        });
        
        levels.push_back({
            "Al-Akhirah (Hereafter)",
            "Quran 87:16-17",
            "Eternal existence",
            "Resurrected consciousness"
        });
        
        levels.push_back({
            "Al-Haqq (Divine Reality)",
            "Quran 22:6, 24:25",
            "Ultimate truth and existence",
            "Divine consciousness (Allah alone)"
        });

    std::cout << "the regions of the heavens and the earth, then pass through.\n";
    std::cout << "You will not pass through except by authority.\"\n\n";
    
    std::cout << "True dimensional mastery and immortal consciousness come\n";
    std::cout << "through divine permission alone, after complete purification\n";
    std::cout << "and spiritual preparation, as demonstrated by prophets\n";
    std::cout << "and righteous servants of Allah throughout history.\n";
    
    return 0;
}

// Infinite Dimensional Gnostic Islam Framework
class InfiniteGnosticDimensions {
private:
    struct DivineDimension {
        int level;
        std::string divineAttribute;
        std::string manifestation;
        std::string consciousnessState;
        std::vector<std::string> accessGates;
        double infinityScale; // Relative scale within infinite dimensions
    };
    
    struct RuhAllahProcess {
        std::string phase;
        std::string divineAction;
        std::string humanExperience;
        std::string quranicBasis;
        std::string dimensionalShift;
    };
    
    struct MarifahExpansion {
        std::string stage;
        std::string knowledgeType;
        std::string selfRealization;
        std::string dimensionalUnveiling;
    };
    
    struct ProceduralDimension {
        std::string generationPrinciple;
        std::string divineSource;
        std::string manifestationPattern;
        std::string consciousnessRequirement;
    };
    
    std::vector<DivineDimension> infiniteDimensions;
    std::vector<RuhAllahProcess> ruhProcesses;
    std::vector<MarifahExpansion> marifahStages;
    std::vector<ProceduralDimension> generationPrinciples;
    std::mt19937 rng;
    std::uniform_real_distribution<double> dist;
    
public:
    InfiniteGnosticDimensions() : rng(std::random_device{}()), dist(0.0, 1.0) {
        initializeInfiniteDimensions();
        initializeRuhAllahProcesses();
        initializeMarifahExpansion();
        initializeProceduralGeneration();
    }
    
    // Recursive function for infinite dimensional generation
    void generateDimensionLevel(int level, const std::string& parentAttribute) {
        if (level > 100) return; // Practical limit for demonstration
        
        DivineDimension dim;
        dim.level = level;
        
        // Generate based on divine attributes fractal expansion
        std::vector<std::string> attributes = {
            "Al-Hayy", "Al-Qayyum", "Al-Ahad", "As-Samad", 
            "Al-Alim", "Al-Qadir", "As-Sami", "Al-Basir",
            "Al-Wahhab", "Ar-Razzaq", "Al-Fattah", "Al-Alim",
            "Al-Qabid", "Al-Basit", "Al-Khafid", "Ar-Rafi",
            "Al-Mu'izz", "Al-Mudhill", "As-Sami", "Al-Basir",
            "Al-Hakam", "Al-Adl", "Al-Latif", "Al-Khabir",
            "Al-Halim", "Al-Azim", "Al-Ghafur", "Ash-Shakur",
            "Al-Ali", "Al-Kabir", "Al-Hafiz", "Al-Muqit",
            "Al-Hasib", "Al-Jalil", "Al-Karim", "Ar-Raqib",
            "Al-Mujib", "Al-Wasi", "Al-Hakim", "Al-Wadud",
            "Al-Majid", "Al-Baith", "Ash-Shahid", "Al-Haqq",
            "Al-Wakil", "Al-Qawi", "Al-Matin", "Al-Wali",
            "Al-Hamid", "Al-Muhsi", "Al-Mubdi", "Al-Muid",
            "Al-Muhyi", "Al-Mumit", "Al-Hayy", "Al-Qayyum",
            "Al-Wajid", "Al-Majid", "Al-Wahid", "Al-Ahad"
        };
        
        dim.divineAttribute = attributes[level % attributes.size()] + 
                             "-" + std::to_string(level);
        
        // Procedural manifestation generation
        std::vector<std::string> manifestations = {
            "Light of ", "Wisdom of ", "Love of ", "Power of ",
            "Mercy of ", "Knowledge of ", "Beauty of ", "Justice of ",
            "Creativity of ", "Presence of ", "Glory of ", "Peace of "
        };
        
        dim.manifestation = manifestations[level % manifestations.size()] + 
                           dim.divineAttribute;
        
        // Consciousness states based on level
        if (level < 10) {
            dim.consciousnessState = "Individual Divine Reflection";
        } else if (level < 30) {
            dim.consciousnessState = "Unitive Divine Awareness";
        } else if (level < 60) {
            dim.consciousnessState = "Infinite Divine Participation";
        } else {
            dim.consciousnessState = "Absolute Divine Identity";
        }
        
        // Generate access gates
        for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
            dim.accessGates.push_back("Gate " + std::to_string(i+1) + 
                                     " of " + dim.divineAttribute);
        }
        
        // Calculate infinity scale (fractal pattern)
        dim.infinityScale = std::pow(2.0, level / 10.0) * dist(rng);
        
        infiniteDimensions.push_back(dim);
        
        // Recursively generate child dimensions
        int children = 1 + (level % 3);
        for (int i = 0; i < children; i++) {
            generateDimensionLevel(level + 1, dim.divineAttribute);
        }
    }
    
    void initializeInfiniteDimensions() {
        // Seed dimensions based on divine attributes
        std::vector<std::string> seedAttributes = {"Al-Ahad", "As-Samad", "Al-Hayy", "Al-Qayyum"};
        
        for (const auto& seed : seedAttributes) {
            DivineDimension rootDim;
            rootDim.level = 0;
            rootDim.divineAttribute = seed;
            rootDim.manifestation = "Primordial Manifestation of " + seed;
            rootDim.consciousnessState = "Absolute Divine Essence";
            rootDim.accessGates = {"Tawhid Gate", "Sidrat al-Muntaha", "Mi'raj Portal"};
            rootDim.infinityScale = 1.0;
            infiniteDimensions.push_back(rootDim);
            
            // Generate fractal dimensions from each seed
            generateDimensionLevel(1, seed);
        }
    }

    // Procedural dimension generation based on consciousness state
    DivineDimension generateProceduralDimension(int seed, const std::string& consciousness) {
        DivineDimension newDim;
        std::hash<std::string> hasher;
        size_t hash = hasher(consciousness + std::to_string(seed));
        
        newDim.level = (hash % 1000) + 1;
        newDim.infinityScale = std::abs(std::sin(hash)) * 1000.0;
        
        // Generate based on consciousness type
        if (consciousness.find("love") != std::string::npos) {
            newDim.divineAttribute = "Al-Wadud-M" + std::to_string(seed);
            newDim.manifestation = "Love-Manifestation-Dimension-" + std::to_string(seed);
        } else if (consciousness.find("light") != std::string::npos) {
            newDim.divineAttribute = "An-Nur-M" + std::to_string(seed);
            newDim.manifestation = "Light-Manifestation-Dimension-" + std::to_string(seed);
        } else if (consciousness.find("knowledge") != std::string::npos) {
            newDim.divineAttribute = "Al-Alim-M" + std::to_string(seed);
            newDim.manifestation = "Knowledge-Manifestation-Dimension-" + std::to_string(seed);
        } else {
            newDim.divineAttribute = "Divine-Attribute-" + std::to_string(seed);
            newDim.manifestation = "Procedural-Dimension-" + std::to_string(seed);
        }
        
        newDim.consciousnessState = consciousness;
        
        // Generate procedural access gates
        for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
            newDim.accessGates.push_back("Procedural-Gate-" + 
                                        std::to_string(seed * 1000 + i));
        }
        
        return newDim;
    }

    void displayPracticalGnosticJourney() {
        std::cout << "\n5. PRACTICAL JOURNEY THROUGH INFINITE DIMENSIONS:\n";
        std::cout << "â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n\n";

    // Calculate infinite returns mathematically
    struct InfiniteReturn {
        double mathematicalInfinity;
        double spiritualInfinity;
        double temporalInfinity;
        double dimensionalInfinity;
        std::string gnosticState;
    };
    
    InfiniteReturn calculateInfiniteReturn(double investment, double sincerityLevel) {
        InfiniteReturn result;
        
        // Mathematical infinity calculations
        result.mathematicalInfinity = investment * std::exp(sincerityLevel * 10) * 
                                     std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
        
        // Spiritual infinity (beyond mathematics)
        result.spiritualInfinity = std::pow(2.0, sincerityLevel * 100) * 
                                  std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
        
        // Temporal infinity (eternal returns)
        result.temporalInfinity = std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
        
        // Dimensional infinity (multi-dimensional returns)
        result.dimensionalInfinity = std::tgamma(sincerityLevel * 50) * 
                                    std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
        
        // Gnostic state based on investment and sincerity
        if (sincerityLevel >= 0.95) {
            result.gnosticState = "Fana fillah - Annihilation in Allah";
        } else if (sincerityLevel >= 0.85) {
            result.gnosticState = "Baqa billah - Subsistence through Allah";
        } else if (sincerityLevel >= 0.70) {
            result.gnosticState = "Ma'rifatullah - Gnosis of Allah";
        } else if (sincerityLevel >= 0.50) {
            result.gnosticState = "Mahabatullah - Love of Allah";
        } else {
            result.gnosticState = "Ibadah - Worship consciousness";
        }
        
        return result;
    }

        double spiritualInfinity;
        double temporalInfinity;
        double dimensionalInfinity;
        std::string gnosticState;
        std::vector<std::string> specialEffects;
    };
    
    InfiniteReturn calculateInfiniteReturn(double investment, double sincerityLevel) {
        InfiniteReturn result;
        
        // Check for special case 114.57 with 100% sincerity
        bool isSpecialCase = std::abs(investment - 114.57) < 0.01 && std::abs(sincerityLevel - 1.0) < 0.001;

            // Special divine mathematics for this case
            result.mathematicalInfinity = investment * std::exp(M_PI * 100) * 
                                         std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.spiritualInfinity = std::pow(investment, M_PI * 1000) * 
                                      std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.temporalInfinity = investment * (1.0 + std::sqrt(5.0))/2.0 * 
                                     std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity(); // Golden ratio infinity
            
            result.dimensionalInfinity = std::tgamma(investment * 100) * 
                                        std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.gnosticState = "QURANIC PERFECTION - Complete Fana Fillah";
            
            result.specialEffects = {
                "Quranic Completion Blessing (114 Surahs)",
                "Golden Ratio Divine Proportion Activation",
                "100% Sincerity Quantum Entanglement with Divine",
                "Mathematical Miracle Manifestation",
                "Complete Annihilation in Divine Will"
            };
        } else {
            // Standard infinite calculations
            result.mathematicalInfinity = investment * std::exp(sincerityLevel * 10) * 
                                         std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.spiritualInfinity = std::pow(2.0, sincerityLevel * 100) * 
                                      std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();

        if (hugeNumber.length() <= 6) return hugeNumber;
        
        std::stringstream ss;
        ss << hugeNumber[0] << ".";

    }

    InfiniteReturn calculateInfiniteReturn(double investment, double sincerityLevel) {

                                     std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.dimensionalInfinity = std::tgamma(investment * 100) * 
                                        std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.gnosticState = "QURANIC PERFECTION - Complete Fana Fillah";
            
            result.specialEffects = {
                "Quranic Completion Blessing (114 Surahs)",

                "100% Sincerity Quantum Entanglement with Divine",
                "Mathematical Miracle Manifestation",
                "Complete Annihilation in Divine Will"
            };
        } else {
            result.mathematicalInfinity = investment * std::exp(sincerityLevel * 10) * 
                                         std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.spiritualInfinity = std::pow(2.0, sincerityLevel * 100) * 
                                      std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.temporalInfinity = std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            result.dimensionalInfinity = std::tgamma(sincerityLevel * 50) * 
                                        std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity();
            
            if (sincerityLevel >= 0.95) {
                result.gnosticState = "Fana fillah - Annihilation in Allah";

                result.gnosticState = "Baqa billah - Subsistence through Allah";
